I cannot even fathom the idea of calling or coming here again. Have you ever had bad customer service? Want to feel like all your questions will be given the fun around? Want to feel frustrated and be given the wrong information? Well look no further come on in to Sutter urgent care in Sacramento! The front desk people are horrid. They have absolutely NO CUSTOMER SERVICE both on the phone AND in person. I am going into a procedure soon and I needed to get covid testing done the coordinator for the surgery called this place to inquire if I needed to get an appt for the testing they advise her no it's just walk in. She called twice And I called as well and was advised to walk in. I get in then BOOM they tell me I NEED AN APPOINTMENT. And I'm like...what?! By this time I'm frustrated.

Want to feel like your not welcome? Want to witness the worst customer service ever? Well come on in to Sutter urgent care! You could tell that they do not like their job and they are not willing to help you. After they told me that I had to schedule an appointment literally MID CONVERSATION she turns to her computer and start typing away! IGNORING ME! I cant believe that Sutter would hire anyone like this to make people feel unwanted and unwelcome.

After a few hours I try to call and literally it would ring and then hang up. I tried calling several times and it would keep doing this. Were the front desk people hanging up on me? A high chance, yes. I've already witnessed their horrible customer service where would the benefit of the doubt be for them not to be? So now I'm frustrated because I can't even get through. I email the surgery coordinator to let her know of their changes and that I might not be able to get in before my procedure. FINALLY I get through to someone and look and behold! Their phone etiquette is also garbage! I tell her that I wanted to schedule an appointment for covid testing for a procedure and she asks when and I say next week Wednesday (I'm calling on a Friday). She says that I needed to schedule the next week because I'm going to need to quarantine. I tell her I understand and I'm wanting to schedule for Saturday. THEN she tells me that I HAVE TO call on Sunday to schedule for Monday. I've already made accommodations for me to quarantine so why do I have to wait?!

BUT, I needed to do my due diligence in trying to schedule an appt. So, I wait and I call Sunday. By this time I've already thrown all hope that I would get someone pleasant on the phone. Which is good because I didn't get anyone pleasant on the phone. If anything I probably got the same person who just turned away when I was talking to her when I was physically in the office. So I explain my situation to the lady over the phone telling her I've been given wrong information, I've been given the runaround of everything, and you know what this woman says. "We try to accommodate all the surgeons here in Sacramento so we're really busy. If you wanted to schedule an appointment you should have called right at opening. 20 people called and they got scheduled." Excuse me? Now your turning the blame on me? <text>I was admitted quickly upon arrival, waiting only around 15 minutes.  It was pretty crowded too, so I was surprised.  Once I was admitted I only waited a few minutes in the exam room before the doctor came in.

< review>
Very impressed with the whole staff from the moment I walked in the door. I was addressed as soon as I came in. I like that they had two sign in counters. I waited only  5 minutes before they gave me new patient paperwork. I appreciated the areas that were highlighted to help me know what was most important for me to fill out. I LOVED the portion that they had printed out on my paperwork with my regular information already printed on it ( like my name, etc ) so I didn't have to write in more than needed. I waited only 5 minutes after my paperwork was given back to the receptionist to go in and see the doctor. When the doctor came in he was very personable, great listener, open minded, and professional. I couldn't imagine a better experience for me or my teenage son. I highly recommend this doctor and won't hesitate to go back again if I need him in the future. Again...awesome staff!!< /review>

< Text>

The apartment itself is kind of okay. Not the greatest equipment (ie washer is very small, fridge is old).

Advertise a gym, a pool, and a tennis court. Gym is actually not bad but ALMOST NEVER accessible because it can only be entered through the gate to the swimming pool and the swimming pool is closed most of the time. In the past few weeks, pool has been closed about 75% of the time which means the gym has also been closed.

Tennis court is advertised -- it sucks. The surface is terrible and there is no wire fence on one side so get ready to hit balls into cars or other apartments.  The lights are ineffective in illuminating the court.

There is an 'activity center' with weights that is open 24/7 but it has only one elliptical machine (creaky and old) and only one stationary bike (which does not work).

The staff is nice but these issues don't get resolved despite requests.<//text>

<Resp>None</Resp><Pictures>None< /Pictures><gmap_id>0x809ae43fef5ad5a7:0x10211b52223940a9<//gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
< review>
This place is pretty nice. My husband and I have lived here for just under two years. The views are amazing as it is right next to the American River Trail, and the gardeners work hard to keep the grounds beautiful.

The units themselves vary wildly, even within a single building, and a 2 bed 2 bath in building 2 could cost more or less than one in building 25, for instance. This is the same across the board. You can ask to see your unit before move in, but in both units we've rented, we didn't see the unit before getting our keys, despite asking a ridiculous, even pestering number of times. That is frustrating.

Moving around the complex is easy as there are several inter-complex trails as well as entry points along the ART. Both pools are crystal clear, and the activity center is a fun place to hang out, especially if it's just your group. There is a massive wood deck there that would be great for large parties as well.

The neighborhood is pretty quiet. You can absolutely hear the noise from East Bidwell and Blue Ravine, unless you're in the back corner by buildings 19-25. However, growing up next to Madison Ave, this is pleasant background noise usually.

The office staff is pretty okay. If they see you coming up the trail they'll pre-fetch your package for you. They're also pretty quick on maintenance. Don't bother with the phone system, it will never get answered, always call or visit the office directly. The maintenance workers (at least for building 1-5 and 25-30) are super friendly and will stop on their golf carts to see if you need anything. There is absolutely an attitude of new money is more important than already paying money, which is frustrating, but we put up with it because it's so beautiful and quiet here.

The other great thing is that it's walking distance from things like Peet's, Target, CVS, Chipotle, an urgent Care center, and a few fast food restaurants. So it gives the area an even more old-town homey feel that my husband and I love.

I would recommend living here if you can afford it. We have one of the cheapest available 3bed/2bath, and with a small dog, we are paying around $1800 a month. It's not cheap to live here, but there are also much more expensive places to live in Folsom. My husband and I are more than happy to call this place home.</review>

<rate>2< /rate><text>I definitely wouldn't recommend renting here; this is not the "luxuary" apartments that they advertise! At best it is an overpriced, mismanaged, (though pretty) college dorm.

The gyms were under construction for much of the time I was here and the tennis court/ golf course are in a sad state of disrepair. The management in the leasing office is exceptionally RUDE and INCOMPETENT --prefering to point fingers rather than address issues. The website is horribly maintained, though they want everything to be managed from there (probably so that the rude management staff don't have to do any face to face work with the tenants.) The culture of the property has the feel of a college dormitory with cars racing in and out of the parking lots at full speed, loud parties spewing forth inconsiderate drunks until 3am, tenants who stomp/ yell constantly in their apartments and others who leave huge piles of dog poop and garbage  sitting right next to waste disposal bins. The property is also extremely wasteful and was constantly watering all summer, despite constant warnings across California about the seriousness of the drought AND their own property signs saying that they were conserving water. The units themselves have all of the trappings of a luxuary apartment but upon close inspection look as though they were put together by a high do-it-yourselfer. Finally, the pricing --while comparative to other luxuary communities in the area at first signing-- goes up astronomically after the first lease is up, increasing to at least 20% of market value.

Overall Overlook at Blue Ravine doean't even remotely live up to its own hype. The only really positive mentions about this property are the pools (they just put in a new one), the maintenance staff (usually friendly and quick), Sarah in the leasing office (she is a gem and deserves a better job) and the walking paths which are admittedly beautiful. NONE of these things make up for the: negatives about the other tenants, the blantant lying about the properties eco-friendly practices, the shoddy craftsmanship in the units, the price or the aweful experience with management. Do yourself a favor and find another complex.< /text>< pictures>

< Review>
I've been a Bell Pest Control customer for years. Four months ago I moved out of state. When I called to cancel and when someone reached out to me about an upcoming service - I was told that the cancellation must be done in writing, mail a letter. In the craze of two moves in the past four months I didn't send the letter, totally spaced. So today Bell called to collect on the service that they've been providing to a vacant house. My card on file wasn't working. I informed their employee that I moved and have a local bank. I just got something in the mail from them yesterday that I hadn't opened. As we talked, I opened a bill. I reiterated that I moved in July. The employee shared that there is no way that Bell could have known that I moved if I didn't submit that information in writing. I told her that I would make the payment but it's not accurate to say that Bell didn't know that I moved. If I've told two separate employees that I moved, I've made Bell aware. Saying that the contract requires that I make the request in writing is factual - I assume. I've been a customer for years and wouldn't begin to know where to find a contract - which is why I did not contest making the payment. However, insisting that because a letter was not received, there was no way to know is not factual. And insisting to reiterate that point made for a very poor customer service experience - for no reason, I already agreed to pay. I didn't contest the payment but shared that I was annoyed and would be sure to share that dissatisfaction. Never raised my voice, didn't even change tone. And from there the service experience went further downhill fast.

The most unbelievable part of the conversation? When I shared that I would pay the $154.00 reflected on my bill today and would follow up with a the late fees at a later date and was told that I can't demand not to pay. Wait, I have to ask permission to call back to pay the late fee? Who is the customer here. Again, didn't contest it, just said I would take care of the $154 reflected on my bill today and the balance at another time (I couldn't reconcile how a bill postmarked 10/23 with no late fees has now accrued two late fees. I figured it was better to see it on a bill.). I have never experienced such terse service from Bell. Until today, everyone whom I have ever worked with has been kind. Solicitors regularly approached with competing offers. I never even entertained a conversation about switching.

I will drop a letter in the mail reflecting my cancellation as I recognize that my phone call and this note do not constitute a cancellation. Guess we could draw further that this until that until the letter is received "Bell would have no way of knowing that I've moved.". Disappointing to see my loyalty to Bell hold so little value.</Review>

< text>
I have had Bell Pest Control Service since I purchased my first home in 2014. I recently purchased a new home in February and within the first month I had a large ant infestation in my home after an ant nest was disturbed following yard work that was done before I purchased the home. I haven't had to do any work in the yard yet, so it wasn't me:-) I called the office first thing in the morning hoping someone could come that day before the ants made it into my pantry. I wish I could remember the name of who I spoke with. She was absolutely lovely, sympathetic and went above and beyond to get techs to my house that afternoon. If I recall, she mentioned that she lives in Galt, I hope that helps her supervisor identify her.
Osmand and Isiah arrived that afternoon to spray inside and out, inspected my attic to make sure there were no rodents (as the home inspection noted some old droppings up there) and they inspected the backyard to see where the ants were coming from. Sure enough, Isiah was able to identify the source and followed the ant trail clear across my backyard to my fruit trees. They treated the area and walked me through everything they did before leaving. We set up a follow-up appointment for Osmand to return two-weeks later to check on the bait he placed in the attic and check on the ant situation.
At our follow-up appointment I informed Osmand that I thought there may be a dead rodent in my wall and I had been smelling it since the day I moved in, he also smelt it. He went straight to the attic, checked the old bait and placed an odor absorption bag in my attic to help with the odor as he couldn't find the animal. OMG it has only been an hour and the smell is already improving. He treated the backyard again as there was still a decent ant trail moving along my patio, but luckily no more ants in the house!! WOOHOO
In my opinion, Bell Pest Control is great. I have always lucked out getting truly amazing techs that seem to go above and beyond. They are always so professional, personable and genuine.
Thank You
Alicia< /text>
